          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





Analysis:



<span class="line"><!---->Analysis:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





(1) _mm256_castsi128_si256 [0] is used to convert a __m128i vector (loaded from iscan_ptr) to a __m256i vector (stored in iscan). Here, the low 128 bits of the converted vector are the same as the original vector, while the high 128 bits are uninitialized (possibly any value).



<span class="line"><!---->(1) _mm256_castsi128_si256 [0] is used to convert a __m128i vector (loaded from iscan_ptr) to a __m256i vector (stored in iscan). Here, the low 128 bits of the converted vector are the same as the original vector, while the high 128 bits are uninitialized (possibly any value).<!----></span>



<br>

Looking at the assembly, in the debug build the final value for the ymm register containing iscan_ptr and the undefined bits is done with vmovaps from the stack (after loading the iscan_ptr bits to a xmm register, then storing it).



<span class="line"><!---->Looking at the assembly, in the debug build the final value for the ymm register containing iscan_ptr and the undefined bits is done with vmovaps from the stack (after loading the iscan_ptr bits to a xmm register, then storing it).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In a release build, in most cases, the load should be done directly to a xmm register with vmovdqu whose ymm mapped value is then used in vpand. In this case the upper half of the register will be zeroed [1].



<span class="line"><!---->In a release build, in most cases, the load should be done directly to a xmm register with vmovdqu whose ymm mapped value is then used in vpand. In this case the upper half of the register will be zeroed [1].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://cdrdv2-public.intel.com/671241/253667-sdm-vol-2b.pdf



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://cdrdv2-public.intel.com/671241/253667-sdm-vol-2b.pdf"><!---->https://cdrdv2-public.intel.com/671241/253667-sdm-vol-2b.pdf<!----></a>



<br>





 To move integer data to and from unaligned memory



<span class="line"><!----> To move integer data to and from unaligned memory<!----></span>



<br>





locations, use the VMOVDQU instruction.



<span class="line"><!---->locations, use the VMOVDQU instruction.<!----></span>



<br>





128-bit Legacy SSE version: Bits (MAXVL-1:128) of the corresponding ZMM destination register remain



<span class="line"><!---->128-bit Legacy SSE version: Bits (MAXVL-1:128) of the corresponding ZMM destination register remain<!----></span>



<br>





unchanged.



<span class="line"><!---->unchanged.<!----></span>



<br>





VEX.128 encoded version: Bits (MAXVL-1:128) of the destination register are zeroed.



<span class="line"><!---->VEX.128 encoded version: Bits (MAXVL-1:128) of the destination register are zeroed.<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
